ODYSSEY -> UMBRIEL MEDIEVAL OVERHAUL
COMPLETE DEF, LANGUAGE AND RETHEME AUDIT
============================================================

STATUS
------
Planning document only. No Odyssey patch or new mod has been implemented yet.

Installed source:
  D:\Steam\steamapps\common\RimWorld\Data\Odyssey
  Version.txt: RimWorld 1.6.4871 rev590
  Runtime log supplied by the user: RimWorld 1.6.4871 rev591

Inventory:
  231 Def XML files
  1,607 concrete Def entries
  67 named XML inheritance templates
  119 concrete XML Def element types
  12 English Keyed LanguageData files
  361 Keyed LanguageData entries (360 unique keys)
  Official duplicate: FishPopulation occurs in ITabs.xml and Misc_Gameplay.xml
  Odyssey has no English DefInjected folder; labels and descriptions stored in
  the Def XML are therefore included directly with every Def below.

IMPORTANT PATCHING RULES
------------------------
1. Keep all vanilla Odyssey defNames unchanged. Odyssey C# code, quests, saves,
   map generation and other mods refer to those names.
2. Override visible labels and descriptions with DefInjected LanguageData where
   possible. Patch fields embedded inside comps, quest rules and letters with
   XML only where DefInjected cannot reach them.
3. Replace texPath, uiIconPath, sounds, effects, costs, stuff categories and
   selected comps without copying entire vanilla Defs.
4. Prefix genuinely new content with Umbriel_, for example Umbriel_CapturedSoul,
   Umbriel_SoulSpinner and Umbriel_CompIngenium.
5. The proposals below are design suggestions, not automatic final English.
   Entries marked TECHNICAL should normally keep their internal name.

LORE BASIS
----------
Umbriel is a floating island held inside a pocket realm of Oblivion. Its city
combines rock, suspended castles, living tree systems and spun-glass structures.
The new Ingenium consumes mortal souls to sustain the city. The Fringe Gyre's
trees produce food and materials; the Kitchens process physical and spiritual
essences; the Lower Middens recycle refuse; proforms grow replacement bodies for
Umbrielians; and soul-spinners gather souls.

The first Ingenium was devised by Vuhon and Sul to hold Baar Dau above Vivec
City after Vivec's disappearance. Its soul bargain was tied to Clavicus Vile.
Umbriel later used a new Ingenium to keep the entire city aloft.

Reference summaries:
  https://en.uesp.net/wiki/Lore:Umbriel
  https://en.uesp.net/wiki/Lore:Ingenium

VISUAL DIRECTION
----------------
- Foundations: irregular dark volcanic stone crossed by pale green or violet
  living roots, rather than metallic deck plating.
- Walls: stone and root masonry. GravshipHull currently accepts only Metallic;
  patch stuffCategories to Stony or make it non-stuffable with a dedicated
  rootstone texture while retaining isAirtight for the underlying mechanic.
- Ingenium: black stone, brass/Dunmer geometry, a bright soul vortex and glass
  conduits. It should feel occult and architectural, not like a machine.
- Motive spires: root-and-glass obelisks that vector the Ingenium's field. They
  replace visible rocket thrusters without changing the required Thruster role.
- Soul cisterns: hanging glass vessels or stone wells containing luminous souls.
- City structures: rock buildings, castles suspended by cables, spun-glass rim
  towers, Hist-like trees, red granite worktops, ovens, hot-stone pits, hanging
  cages and the organic Lower Middens.
- Orbit maps: reinterpret as Umbriel's surrounding Oblivion bubble. Replace
  starfield/metal-platform art with mist, floating rock, roots and glass.

SOUL-FUEL MECHANIC
------------------
Recommended architecture:

A. New resources
   Umbriel_LesserSoul       animal or weak creature soul
   Umbriel_CommonSoul       large/sentient non-human soul
   Umbriel_BlackSoul        humanlike mortal soul
   Umbriel_SoulGemEmpty     optional capture vessel

   Each soul item receives a FuelValue stat. The existing ChemfuelTank and
   LargeChemfuelTank CompRefuelable filters can then be patched to accept only
   these soul items. This reuses Odyssey's normal range and launch-fuel logic.

B. Capturing souls
   Add an Umbriel_SoulSpinner building or creature. When an eligible pawn dies
   on a map containing an active soul-spinner or the Ingenium, a custom death
   listener creates the appropriate captured-soul item. A stricter TES mode can
   require a Soul Snare/Soul Trap hediff at the moment of death.

C. Deliberate sacrifice
   Add an Ingenium gizmo or ritual that targets a prisoner, slave or consenting
   colonist. Completion kills the pawn and transfers a black soul directly to
   the Ingenium. It must count as a hostile/organ-harvesting-style act where
   appropriate and generate memories, history events and ideology reactions.

D. Continuous upkeep
   Add Umbriel_CompIngenium to GravEngine. It drains soul value from linked soul
   cisterns every day, persists its state in saves and blocks launch when starved.
   Suggested escalation:
     0-1 day empty: warning and Ingenium glow/sound weakens
     1-3 days empty: power/ward failures and negative mood
     3+ days empty: configurable structural damage or forced crash incident
   Do not destroy the map immediately without a warning and grace period.

E. Launch consumption
   Keep Odyssey's range calculation. Soul cisterns replace chemfuel tanks, so
   distance consumes soul value naturally. The custom Ingenium component should
   perform one additional pre-flight validation for its upkeep reserve.

F. Initial balance draft
   Lesser soul: 5 fuel
   Common soul: 25 fuel
   Black soul: 100 fuel
   Ingenium upkeep: 25 fuel/day
   Exact values require playtesting against Odyssey's fuel-per-tile formula.

G. Compatibility
   Keep ThingDef names such as GravEngine and ChemfuelTank. Only their presentation
   and selected comps change. This preserves Odyssey code and compatibility with
   mods that search for vanilla Defs.

IMPLEMENTATION PHASES
---------------------
1. Text-only terminology patch and construction material/cost changes.
2. Rootstone, wall, Ingenium, cistern, spire, veil and skiff textures.
3. Captured-soul Defs, soul-spinner, sacrifice workflow and CompIngenium DLL.
4. Quest/site conversion: gravcore hunt becomes recovery of Ingenium shards.
5. Oblivion-space conversion, Daedric enemies and Umbriel-specific inhabitants.
6. Optional compatibility with medieval content mods and fantasy race mods.

PROPOSAL TAGS
-------------
REPLACE    Concrete new identity, label or asset proposed.
REWRITE    Text/quest should be rewritten around Umbriel.
RETEXTURE  Mechanics can stay; medieval/Umbriel art is needed.
KEEP       Already suitable for a medieval fantasy environment.
TECHNICAL  Internal helper; keep the defName and retheme referenced content.
OPTIONAL   Broader conversion not required for the Umbriel core.

They are a common sight on deep-space stations and interstellar ships, where genetic modification is often a more cost-effective solution than upgrading spacecraft to support unaltered human physiology.

  Proposal: [REPLACE] Ingenium — soul-powered occult heart of Umbriel; new texture and CompIngenium.
  Vanilla description: The ultratech heart of a gravship. The grav engine generates lift by inverting and intensifying the effect of gravity in a field around itself. This engine can lift upwards, but does not produce forward thrust. It can't function far from a large gravity well like a planet, so it is useless for interplanetary travel.\n\nWhen launched, anything on substructure that's connected to the grav engine will be transported to a new map. Without a grav anchor, launching a gravship will abandon your current map.\n\nGlitterworld engineers use gravships to launch orbital platforms and build skyrippers. They require massive and hyper-specialized facilities to produce, making them a rare sight outside of glitterworlds.

===============================================================================
SECTION 3 — AUDIT RESULT AND RECOMMENDED MOD BOUNDARY
===============================================================================

Concrete Def proposal totals:
  REPLACE:    302
  REWRITE:    357
  RETEXTURE:   47
  KEEP:       354
  TECHNICAL:  512
  OPTIONAL:    35
  TOTAL:    1,607

LanguageData totals:
  terminology-first Umbriel drafts: 143
  manual semantic rewrites:          46
  keep candidates:                  172
  TOTAL:                             361

Recommended mod identity:
  Name: Umbriel — The Infernal City
  Package ID example: Matthias.UmbrielOdyssey
  Required DLC: Ludeon.RimWorld.Odyssey
  Optional dependency: OskarPotocki.VFE.Medieval2 for compatible medieval assets

Do not make this a hidden FIP-Sunset load folder. It is a complete Elder Scrolls
conversion with its own art, mechanics and identity. FIP-Sunset currently only
contains a LoadFolders.xml reference to Medieval2_Odyssey; the actual folder had
no content and was removed during empty-folder cleanup.

Compatibility warning:
  FIP-Repconn and this Umbriel overhaul both reinterpret the same Odyssey Defs
  and English strings. They should be declared incompatible, or the Umbriel mod
  must load last and intentionally overwrite every REPCONN/Hellion term.

Recommended first implementation slice:
  1. GravEngine, Substructure, GravshipHull and all linked facilities.
  2. Gravcore, GravlitePanel, Vacstone and relevant research.
  3. All gravship/orbit Keyed LanguageData and DefInjected text.
  4. Soul resources, soul cistern fuel filters and CompIngenium.
  5. Only then convert quests, space sites, enemies and the rest of Odyssey.

Open design choices before implementation:
  - Soul capture: automatic Ingenium radius, explicit Soul Trap, or both.
  - Starvation consequence: launch lock only, escalating damage, or eventual crash.
  - Whether human sacrifice is mandatory or merely the fastest source.
  - Whether orbit remains a magical pocket layer or is removed from the setting.
  - Whether Daedric constructs reuse mechanoid bodies temporarily or receive
    entirely new races and textures from the first release.

END OF AUDIT
